country_event = {

    id = 31716
    title = "EVTNAME31716" #Eiffel Tower Construction
    desc = "EVTDESC31716"
    picture = "eiffel_tower_construction"

	fire_only_once = yes
    is_triggered_only = yes

    option = {
        name = "EVT31716OPTA"
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 40000 }
                    NOT = { check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 1 } }
                }
            }
            owner = { set_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 40 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 40000 }
                    check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 9 }
                }
            }
            owner = { change_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 40 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { money = 40000 } }
            owner = { treasury = -40000 }
        }
        random_list = {
            50 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 600 } }
            40 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 730 } }
            10 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 900 } }
        }

        ai_chance = {
            factor = 40
        }
    }

    option = {
        name = "EVT31716OPTB"
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 30000 }
                    NOT = { check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 1 } }
                }
            }
            owner = { set_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 30 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 30000 }
                    check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 9 }
                }
            }
            owner = { change_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 30 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { money = 30000 } }
            owner = { treasury = -30000 }
        }
        random_list = {
            30 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 600 } }
            50 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 730 } }
            20 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 900 } }
        }

        ai_chance = {
            factor = 40
        }
    }
	option = {
        name = "EVT31716OPTC"
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 20000 }
                    NOT = { check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 1 } }
                }
            }
            owner = { set_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 20 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    NOT = { money = 20000 }
                    check_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 9 }
                }

            owner = { change_variable = { which = owed_cash_money value = 20 } }
        }
        random_owned = {
            limit = { owner = { money = 20000 } }
            owner = { treasury = -20000 }
        }
        random_list = {
            30 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 600 } }
            30 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 730 } }
            40 = { add_country_modifier = { name = eiffel_torre_construction duration = 900 } }

country_event = {

    id = 31717
    title = "EVTNAME31717" #Eiffel Tower finished
    desc = "EVTDESC31717"
    picture = "eiffel_tower_finished"
    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
        498 = { is_core = THIS }
        owns = 498
        NOT = {
			THIS = { has_country_modifier = eiffel_torre_construction }
		}
		has_global_flag = the_eiffel_tower_was_built
		has_global_flag = catalan_tower
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }

    option = {
        name = "EVT31717OPTA"
        set_country_flag = eiffel_tower_built
        FRA = {
            set_country_flag = eiffel_tower_built
        }
        498 = {
                set_province_flag = eiffel_tower_built
                add_province_modifier = {
                    name = the_eiffel_tower
                    duration = -1
                }
        }
        prestige = 20
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 31719
    title = "The Urgell Channels Are Finished"
    desc = "The Canal System in the Catalan region of Urgell is finally finished. 6.000 workers and slaves worked on the construction, 1.000 of which died of cholera. The surrounding lands are now irrigable, allowing their agricultural cultivation."
    picture = "urgell_channels"
    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
        500 = { is_core = THIS }
        owns = 500
        NOT = {
			THIS = { has_country_modifier = urgell_channels_construction }
		}
		has_global_flag = urgell_channel_built
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 5 }

    option = {
        name = "Visque!" #Catalan Occidental pronunciation trolling

		500 = {

			add_province_modifier = { name = urgell_channels_built duration = -1 }
        }
		
		ai_chance = {
            factor = 100
        }
    }
}

country_event = {
    id = 31722
    title = "The 1845 Constitution"
    desc = "SPAFORCEDCONSTITUTION"
    picture = "spa_1845_constitution"
    fire_only_once = yes

    trigger = {
        tag = SPA
		has_country_flag = spa_1837_constitution
		year = 1845
		OR = {
			government = hms_government
			government = prussian_constitutionalism
		}
		is_greater_power = no
    }

    mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }

    option = {
        name = "We accept."
        set_country_flag = spa_1845_constitution
		CLN = { add_country_modifier = { name = spain_revolt duration = 365 } }
        prestige = -2
		political_reform = landed_voting
        political_reform = party_appointed
        political_reform = first_past_the_post
        political_reform = no_trade_unions
        political_reform = underground_parties
		CLN = { add_country_modifier = { name = spain_revolt duration = 365 } }
		any_pop = {
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = conservative
				factor = -3
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = reactionary
				factor = -5
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = liberal
				factor = 6
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = socialist
				factor = 7
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = radical
				factor = 8
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
            factor = 99
			modifier = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = liberal 
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = { 
				war_policy = jingoism
				factor = 0
			}
        }
    }
	
	option = {
        name = "We do not accept."
        set_country_flag = rejected_spa_1845_constitution
        prestige = 1
		any_pop = {
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = conservative
				factor = 5
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = reactionary
				factor = 7
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = liberal
				factor = -2
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = socialist
				factor = -2
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				ideology = radical
				factor = -3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
            factor = 1
			modifier = { 
				ruling_party_ideology = liberal 
				factor = 4
			}
			modifier = { 
				war_policy = jingoism
				factor = 0
			}
        }
    }
}

            militancy = 3

        }
		any_pop = { 
			limit = { has_pop_culture = catalan }
			scaled_consciousness = {
				factor = 6
				ideology = liberal

    title = "The Sarawak Demand Limbang"

    is_triggered_only = yes

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 1
		}
    }
	
	option = {
        name = "What about no?"
		prestige = 5
		SWK = { country_event = 18482169 }
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0
		}
    }
}

country_event = {
	id = 18482187
	title = "Claims to Limbang"
	desc = "LIMBANGJESARAWAK"
	picture = "sarawakpointgun4"
    
    fire_only_once = yes
	
    trigger = {
        tag = ENG
		year = 1890
		owns = 3586
		BRU = { owns = 3587 }
    }
	
    mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	option = {
        name = "Marudi is rightfully a part of Sarawak."
		random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    BRU = { vassal_of = THIS }
                }
            }
            owner = {
				3587 = { secede_province = THIS }
			}
        }
		random_owned = {
            limit = {
                owner = {
                    BRU = { OR = { is_vassal = no NOT = { vassal_of = THIS } } }
                }
            }
            owner = {
				BRU = { country_event = 18482188 }
			}
        }
    }
}

			}
		}

			}
			consciousness = -3
		}

			}

		}
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}
